My approach focuses on nominal GDP to reflect the actual dollar value in 2049, which is likely more relevant for future economic size comparisons. Applying a real growth rate of 2.2% to a nominal base may understate the future nominal value if inflation is not accounted for.\\n\\n3. **Refined Growth Assumptions**: Historically, US nominal GDP growth has averaged around 4%\u20135% annually over long periods, driven by real growth (2%\u20133%) and inflation (1.5%\u20132%).
